## üì∞ General changes and notes

Summary of changes here!

<summary>Github Commits :octocat:</summary>
<blockquote>

- chore: changelogs for 5.1
- many updates
- - fix quests typos, rewards, depencencies, etc
- - add a freeze option to start game with frozen ticks
- - remove xycraft recipe for aluminum
- - fix create JEI crash with chocolate pie from farmersdelight
- - add `create_enchantment_industry:experience` to experience tag
- - add `hydrofluoric_acid` to chemthrower to act like water
- Updated PT_BR localization (#3628)
- * Updated PT_BR localization
- * Updated PT_BR localization
- - small fix
- Update zh_cn quest Translation (#3632)
- * resort zh_cn quest translation by original order
- * update zh_cn quest translation
- * update zh_cn quest translation
- * update zh_cn quest chapter
- * update zh_cn quest translation
- Add Compressed recipe for ATM/Vib alloy (#3661)
- Added compression recipes for vibranium_allthemodium_alloy_block from 1x to 7x.
- 
- Each tier multiplies recipe energy √ó3 (but raw crafting would be √ó9), so every tier gives a 66.67% reduction vs making 9 of the previous tier and an exponential cumulative saving vs starting from base blocks.
- For 7x -> 19.68 TFE
- fix: add bee queen to spawners and jar blacklist
- fix: replace bauxite with aluminum at MI quarry
- fix: mekmm recipe error
- fix: update crash assistant config</blockquote>

</details>

<details>
<summary>cobblegengalore/blockgen/create/ochrum</summary>

```diff
+{
+  type: "cobblegengalore:blockgen"
+  result: {
+    id: "create:ochrum"
+    count: 1
+  }
+  speed: 2
+  left: {
+    Name: "minecraft:water"
+  }
+  right: {
+    Name: "minecraft:lava"
+  }
+  modifier: {
+    Name: "create:ochrum"
+  }
+  neoforge:conditions: [
+    {
+      type: "almostunified:conditional"
+      conditions_met: true
+      original_conditions: [
+        {
+          type: "neoforge:mod_loaded"
+          modid: "create"
+        }
+      ]
+    }
+  ]
+}

```


</details>

<summary>create_hypertube/sequenced_assembly/tube_scanner</summary>

```diff
+{
+  type: "create:sequenced_assembly"
+  ingredient: {
+    item: "create_hypertube:redstone_detector_tube_attachment"
+  }
+  loops: 1
+  results: [
+    {
+      chance: 100
+      id: "create_hypertube:tube_scanner_attachment"
+    }
+  ]
+  sequence: [
+    {
+      type: "create:deploying"

+        {
+          item: "create_hypertube:tube_scanner_unfinished"

+          item: "create:brass_sheet"
+        }
+      ]
+      results: [
+        {
+          id: "create_hypertube:tube_scanner_unfinished"

+      ]
+    }

+          item: "create_hypertube:tube_scanner_unfinished"

+        }
```

<summary>create_dragons_plus/filling/dragon_breath</summary>

```diff
 {
   neoforge:conditions: [
     {
       type: "almostunified:conditional"
       conditions_met: true
       original_conditions: [
         {
           type: "create_dragons_plus:config_feature"
           feature: "create_dragons_plus:fluid/dragon_breath"
         }
       ]
     }
   ]
   type: "create:filling"
   ingredients: [
     {
       item: "minecraft:glass_bottle"
     }
     {
-      type: "fluid_stack"
+      type: "neoforge:single"
       amount: 250
       fluid: "create_dragons_plus:dragon_breath"
     }
   ]
   results: [
     {
       id: "minecraft:dragon_breath"
     }
   ]
 }

```

```diff
         }
       ]
     }
   ]

     {

       amount: 250
       fluid: "create_dragons_plus:black_dye"
     }
```

```diff
   group: "whispering_trapdoors"
   pattern: [
-    " A "
-    " A "
-    "ABA"
+    "A"
+    "A"
+    "B"
   ]
   key: {
     A: {
       item: "minecraft:oak_planks"
     }
     B: {
       item: "mcwtrpdoors:print_whispering"
     }
   }
   result: {
-    count: 4
+    count: 1
     id: "mcwtrpdoors:oak_whispering_trapdoor"
   }
 }

```


</details>

<summary>mcwtrpdoors/print_bamboo</summary>

```diff
 {

   pattern: [
     " A "
     "ABA"
     " A "
   ]
   key: {
     B: {
-      item: "minecraft:paper"
+      item: "minecraft:bamboo_trapdoor"
     }
     A: {
-      item: "minecraft:bamboo"
+      item: "minecraft:paper"
     }
   }
   result: {
     count: 4
     id: "mcwtrpdoors:print_bamboo"
   }
 }
```
